SELECT [g].[ID] AS [IdGastosReal], [g].[IDGASTO] AS [IdGasto], [g].[IDPROVEEDOR] AS [IdProveedor], CASE
    WHEN [s].[ID] IS NOT NULL THEN [s].[ID]
    ELSE 0
END AS [IdSegmento], CASE
    WHEN [s].[ID] IS NOT NULL THEN [s].[NOMBRE]
    ELSE ''
END AS [NombreSegmento], [c].[CUENTA] AS [Cuenta], [c].[IDCUENTA] AS [IdCuenta], [g].[MONTO] AS [Monto], COALESCE([g].[FECHA], '0001-01-01') AS [Fecha], [g].[OBSERVACION] AS [Observacion], [g].[ESTADO] AS [Estado], [g].[VENTA] AS [Venta]
FROM [PROYECTO] AS [p]
INNER JOIN [GASTOSEJECUCION] AS [g] ON [p].[ID] = [g].[IDPROYECTO]
INNER JOIN [GASTOS] AS [g0] ON [g].[IDGASTO] = [g0].[ID]
LEFT JOIN [SEGMENTO] AS [s] ON [g].[SEGMENTO] = [s].[ID]
INNER JOIN [CUENTA] AS [c] ON [g0].[IDCUENTA] = [c].[ID]
WHERE [p].[ID] = @__idproyecto_0
ORDER BY CASE
    WHEN ([g].[ESTADO] <> 'Forecast') OR [g].[ESTADO] IS NULL THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
    ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)
END, COALESCE([g].[FECHA], '0001-01-01')

    WHEN [s].[ID] IS NOT NULL THEN [s].[ID]
    ELSE 0
END AS [IdSegmento], CASE
    WHEN [s].[ID] IS NOT NULL THEN [s].[NOMBRE]
    ELSE ''
END AS [NombreSegmento], [c].[CUENTA] AS [Cuenta], [c].[IDCUENTA] AS [IdCuenta], [g].[MONTO] AS [Monto], COALESCE([g].[FECHA], '0001-01-01') AS [Fecha], [g].[OBSERVACION] AS [Observacion], [g].[ESTADO] AS [Estado], [g].[VENTA] AS [Venta]
FROM [PROYECTO] AS [p]
INNER JOIN [GASTOSEJECUCION] AS [g] ON [p].[ID] = [g].[IDPROYECTO]
INNER JOIN [GASTOS] AS [g0] ON [g].[IDGASTO] = [g0].[ID]
LEFT JOIN [SEGMENTO] AS [s] ON [g].[SEGMENTO] = [s].[ID]
INNER JOIN [CUENTA] AS [c] ON [g0].[IDCUENTA] = [c].[ID]
WHERE [p].[ID] = @__idproyecto_0
ORDER BY CASE
    WHEN ([g].[ESTADO] <> 'Forecast') OR [g].[ESTADO] IS NULL THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
    ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)
END, COALESCE([g].[FECHA], '0001-01-01')

SELECT [g].[ID] AS [IdGastosReal], [g].[IDGASTO] AS [IdGasto], [g].[IDPROVEEDOR] AS [IdProveedor], CASE
    WHEN [s].[ID] IS NOT NULL THEN [s].[ID]
    ELSE 0
END AS [IdSegmento], CASE
    WHEN [s].[ID] IS NOT NULL THEN [s].[NOMBRE]
    ELSE ''
END AS [NombreSegmento], [c].[CUENTA] AS [Cuenta], [c].[IDCUENTA] AS [IdCuenta], [g].[MONTO] AS [Monto], COALESCE([g].[FECHA], '0001-01-01') AS [Fecha], [g].[OBSERVACION] AS [Observacion], [g].[ESTADO] AS [Estado], [g].[VENTA] AS [Venta]
FROM [PROYECTO] AS [p]
INNER JOIN [GASTOSEJECUCION] AS [g] ON [p].[ID] = [g].[IDPROYECTO]
INNER JOIN [GASTOS] AS [g0] ON [g].[IDGASTO] = [g0].[ID]
LEFT JOIN [SEGMENTO] AS [s] ON [g].[SEGMENTO] = [s].[ID]
INNER JOIN [CUENTA] AS [c] ON [g0].[IDCUENTA] = [c].[ID]
WHERE [p].[ID] = @__idproyecto_0
ORDER BY CASE
    WHEN ([g].[ESTADO] <> 'Forecast') OR [g].[ESTADO] IS NULL THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
    ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)
END, COALESCE([g].[FECHA], '0001-01-01')
